I am thinking...: Now I have a comprehensive understanding of the plugin/extension loading system in Apache Kafka. Let me compile the complete list of relevant files.

The task asks for files that implement:
1. The PluginClassLoader
2. Plugin scanning via reflection
3. Interface-based dependency injection used for Connector, Converter, and HeaderConverter plugins

The core files are:

**Core isolation/plugin loading package** (all in `connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/`):
1. `PluginClassLoader.java` - The custom classloader for loading plugins in isolation
2. `DelegatingClassLoader.java` - The delegating classloader that manages plugin classloaders
3. `ClassLoaderFactory.java` - Factory for creating classloaders
4. `PluginClassLoaderFactory.java` - Interface for the factory
5. `PluginScanner.java` - Abstract base class for plugin scanning
6. `ReflectionScanner.java` - Reflection-based plugin scanner (uses classgraph)
7. `ServiceLoaderScanner.java` - ServiceLoader-based plugin scanner
8. `Plugins.java` - Main class for plugin management and DI (newConnector, newConverter, newHeaderConverter, etc.)
9. `PluginDesc.java` - Descriptor for a plugin
10. `PluginScanResult.java` - Result of a plugin scan
11. `PluginType.java` - Enum of plugin types
12. `PluginUtils.java` - Utility methods for plugins (shouldLoadInIsolation, pluginSources, etc.)
13. `PluginSource.java` - Represents a source of plugins
14. `PluginDiscoveryMode.java` - Enum for discovery modes
15. `LoaderSwap.java` - Helper for classloader swapping
16. `PluginsRecommenders.java` - Recommenders for plugin configuration
17. `VersionedPluginLoadingException.java` - Exception for versioned plugin loading

## Summary of Findings

The Apache Kafka Connect plugin/extension loading system in `apache/kafka` (repo at `/workspace/kafka--0753c489`) is implemented across these key areas:

### Core Plugin Loading Infrastructure (`connect/runtime/.../isolation/`)
- **`PluginClassLoader.java`** — Child-first `URLClassLoader` that loads plugin classes in isolation; its `loadClass()` uses `PluginUtils.shouldLoadInIsolation()` to decide delegation
- **`DelegatingClassLoader.java`** — Parent classloader managing a registry of `PluginClassLoader` instances; `installDiscoveredPlugins()` populates it from scan results; `loadVersionedPluginClass()` dispatches to the right loader
- **`PluginScanner.java`** — Abstract base for plugin discovery with `discoverPlugins()` entry point
- **`ReflectionScanner.java`** — Uses ClassGraph library to reflectively find all concrete subclasses of plugin interfaces
- **`ServiceLoaderScanner.java`** — Uses `java.util.ServiceLoader` only (modern KIP-898 strategy)
- **`Plugins.java`** — Central DI facade: `newConnector()`, `newConverter()`, `newHeaderConverter()`, `newConfigProvider()`, `withClassLoader()`, etc.
- **`PluginUtils.java`** — `shouldLoadInIsolation()`, `pluginSources()`, `isolatedPluginSource()`, `computeAliases()`
- Plus: `PluginDesc`, `PluginScanResult`, `PluginType`, `PluginSource`, `PluginDiscoveryMode`, `LoaderSwap`, `PluginsRecommenders`, `VersionedPluginLoadingException`, `ClassLoaderFactory`, `PluginClassLoaderFactory`

### Plugin Interfaces (`connect/api/`)
`Connector`, `SourceConnector`, `SinkConnector`, `Converter`, `HeaderConverter`, `Transformation`, `Predicate`, `ConnectorClientConfigOverridePoli

handleLinkageError(PluginType type, PluginSource source, Supplier<U> function) {\n   164          // It's difficult to know for sure if the iterator was able to advance past the first broken\n   165          // plugin class, or if it will continue to fail on that broken class for any subsequent calls\n   166          // to Iterator::hasNext or Iterator::next\n   167          // For reference, see This limit is chosen to be higher than the typical number\n   173          // of plugins in a single plugin location, and to limit the amount of log-spam on startup.\n   174          for (int i = 0; i < 100; i++) {\n   175              try {\n   176                  return function.get();\n   177              } catch (LinkageError t) {\n   178                  // As an optimization, hide subsequent error logs if two consecutive errors look similar.\n   179                  // This reduces log-spam for iterators which cannot advance and rethrow the same exception.\n   180                  if (lastError == null\n   181                          || !Objects.equals(lastError.getClass(), t.getClass())\n   182                          || !Objects.equals(lastError.getMessage(), t.getMessage())) {\n   183                      log.error(\"Failed to discover {} in {}{}\",\n   184                              type.simpleName(), source, reflectiveErrorDescription(t.getCause()), t);\n   185                  }\n   186                  lastError = t;\n   187              }\n   188          }\n   189          log.error(\"Received excessive ServiceLoader errors: assuming the runtime ServiceLoader implementation cannot \" +\n   190                          \"skip faulty implementations.
